[2;36m                    [0m         [39multimately by the fuzz entry point `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/json_fuzz.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The corrupted memory access is a read of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m at an address immediately [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte region.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The allocation in question is made via `malloc` [0m[1;39m([0m[39moperator new[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before parsing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbegins; the overflow happens when processing specific JSON input.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The ASan report shows the exact shadow memory layout and call stack leading to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe crash.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/shadowsocks/src/json.c`, particularly around line [0m[1;36m634[0m[39m in `json_parse_ex`. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Allocation and buffer-size logic used to hold JSON tokens or strings in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Related parsing routines in `json.c` that manage buffer boundaries.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness in `src/json_fuzz.c` as context for how inputs arrive [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mthough it is not the root cause[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The heap-buffer-overflow originates in the Unicode-escape [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\uXXXX`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurrogate-pair [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\uXXXX\uYYYY`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m parsing in json_parse_ex [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/json.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Both [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbranches perform an off-by-one boundary check on the remaining buffer length before[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpre-incrementing `state.ptr` to read hex digits, allowing a read of one byte past [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`end`.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Targeted Fixes[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Single Unicode Escape [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\uXXXX`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Original check at line ~[0m[1;36m306[0m[39m:  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || [0m[35m/[0m[39m* then read [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m × *++state.ptr *[0m[35m/[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Change to ensure at least [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bytes remain [0m[1;39m([0m[39mone for each of the four hex [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits plus one more to stay in-bounds[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m || [0m[35m/[0m[39m* same subsequent tests *[0m[35m/[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Surrogate Pair [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\uXXXX\uYYYY`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Original check at line ~[0m[1;36m323[0m[39m:  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m!='\\' || [0m[33m...[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Change to require at least [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes remain [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbackslash, [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m, plus four hex [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m!='\\' || [0m[33m...[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Open `src/json.c`.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Locate the `case [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m:` block [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m300[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Modify the first boundary check:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```diff[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m ||[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        + if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m ||[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Immediately below, locate the surrogate-pair detection block:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39muchar & [0m[1;36m0xF800[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0xD800[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[39m* current code: if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m || [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        Change its boundary check:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```diff[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != '\\' || [0m[33m...[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        + if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != '\\' || [0m[33m...[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep all subsequent pointer increments, [0m[1;35mhex_value[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m calls, error handling, and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUTF-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m surrogate logic unchanged.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Functionality[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing control flow [0m[1;39m([0m[39merror formatting, `goto e_failed`, surrogate [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetection and combining[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains untouched.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to the fuzzing harness, tests, or external libraries.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This patch strictly tightens buffer-length preconditions, eliminating the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone-byte read-past while preserving correct parsing of valid `\u` sequences.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Verification and Side-Effects[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Recompile and run unit tests and `json_fuzz`. The off-by-one error should no [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlonger trigger AddressSanitizer.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Potential side-effect: Inputs that previously were borderline [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexactly four or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msix bytes remaining[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m now correctly emit an [0m[32m"Invalid character value"[0m[39m error instead [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof overrunning memory.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No broader utility or API behavior is altered.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar boundary checks in JSON libraries [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., jsmn, cJSON[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m always require [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`>= needed_length`, not `> needed_length - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`. Our changes align with this best [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpractice.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Completion[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root-Cause Analysis  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The AddressSanitizer report shows a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read past an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer at [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjson.[0m[1;92mc:634[0m[39m, which corresponds to the null-literal [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`case [0m[32m'n'[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m handler. A closer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlook at all literal branches [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`true`, `false`, `null`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m reveals identical off-by-one[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks: each checks for fewer remaining characters than it actually consumes, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowing exactly-boundary inputs [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `end - state.ptr == [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` in the null case[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mslip through and invoke `++state.ptr` one byte beyond `end`. The earlier patch [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts focused solely on Unicode escapes and thus did not address these literal [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandlers, so the crash remains at the null-literal code.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Patches to Apply  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Literal Handlers  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • In the `case [0m[32m't'[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m branch, change the guard from  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m || …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       to  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • In the `case [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m branch, change the guard from  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       to  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m || …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • In the `case [0m[32m'n'[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m branch, change the guard from  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m || …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       to  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Reapply Unicode-Escape Patches  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m([0m[39mThese were correctly attempted but must be included since we are patching the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitial codebase.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • In the single-`\uXXXX` handler, change  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       to  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m || …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • In the surrogate-pair handler, change  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m || …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       to  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m || …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Open src/json.c.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Locate the three literal branches [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m600[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m620[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m631[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m635[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `case [0m[32m't'[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `case [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `case [0m[32m'n'[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Adjust the `< N` thresholds as specified above.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Locate the Unicode-escape code at the existing patch sites [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m303[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand [0m[1;36m320[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and reapply the `< [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `< [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m` changes.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Rebuild and rerun `json_fuzz` to confirm no heap-buffer-overflow remains.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – We only tighten boundary checks to ensure we never read past `end`.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Invalid or truncated literals were already intended to be rejected via `goto [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39me_unknown_value`; the change only makes the check correct, not more permissive.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Unicode-escape logic remains unchanged in behavior, aside from corrected [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds checks.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigations  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Inputs that end mid-literal [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[32m"tru"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now fail immediately with [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`e_unknown_value` rather than briefly advancing the pointer and crashing; this is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect JSON-error behavior.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – No other branches or utility functions are modified, so impact on unrelated [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality is minimal.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Fuzzing harness and tests remain untouched; existing test suite should pass, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand fuzzing will no longer trigger this out-of-bounds read.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References to Similar Patterns  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
